			<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">Member states of the United Nations</h1>
									<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">
									<div id="siteSub">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
								<div id="contentSub"><span class="mw-redirectedfrom">  (Redirected from <a href="/w/index.php?title=United_Nations_member_states&amp;redirect=no" class="mw-redirect" title="United Nations member states">United Nations member states</a>)</span></div>
												<div id="jump-to-nav" class="mw-jump">
					Jump to:					<a href="#mw-head">navigation</a>, 					<a href="#p-search">search</a>
				</div>
				<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:372px;"><a href="/wiki/File:United_Nations_Members.svg" class="image"><img alt="A political map of the world with all territories shaded blue to denote United Nations membership, except Antarctica, the Palestinian territories, the Vatican, and Western Sahara, which are grey" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/13/United_Nations_Members.svg/370px-United_Nations_Members.svg.png" width="370" height="188" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/13/United_Nations_Members.svg/555px-United_Nations_Members.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/13/United_Nations_Members.svg/740px-United_Nations_Members.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="940" data-file-height="477" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:United_Nations_Members.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Map of the United Nations (UN) member states, with their territories (including <a href="/wiki/Dependent_territory" title="Dependent territory">dependent territories</a>) recognized by the UN in blue<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup></div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:372px;"><a href="/wiki/File:United_Nations_Geneva_2010-07-01.JPG" class="image"><img alt="A long row of flags" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c9/United_Nations_Geneva_2010-07-01.JPG/370px-United_Nations_Geneva_2010-07-01.JPG" width="370" height="247" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c9/United_Nations_Geneva_2010-07-01.JPG/555px-United_Nations_Geneva_2010-07-01.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c9/United_Nations_Geneva_2010-07-01.JPG/740px-United_Nations_Geneva_2010-07-01.JPG 2x" data-file-width="3888" data-file-height="2592" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:United_Nations_Geneva_2010-07-01.JPG" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Flags of the member states of the United Nations, in front of the <a href="/wiki/Palace_of_Nations" title="Palace of Nations">Palace of Nations</a> (<a href="/wiki/Geneva" title="Geneva">Geneva</a>, <a href="/wiki/Switzerland" title="Switzerland">Switzerland</a>). Since 2015, the flags of the two <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_General_Assembly_observers#Non-member_observer_states" title="United Nations General Assembly observers">non-member observer states</a> are raised alongside those of the 193 member states.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The <b>United Nations member states</b> are the 193 <a href="/wiki/Sovereign_states" class="mw-redirect" title="Sovereign states">sovereign states</a> that are members of the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> (UN) and have equal representation in the <a href="/wiki/UN_General_Assembly" class="mw-redirect" title="UN General Assembly">UN General Assembly</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup> The UN is the world's largest intergovernmental organization, ahead of the <a href="/wiki/Organisation_of_Islamic_Cooperation" title="Organisation of Islamic Cooperation">Organisation of Islamic Cooperation</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup></p>
<p><span id="Membership_terms"></span> The criteria for admission of new members to the UN are set out in <a href="/wiki/Chapter_II_of_the_United_Nations_Charter" title="Chapter II of the United Nations Charter">Chapter II</a>, Article 4 of the <a href="/wiki/UN_Charter" class="mw-redirect" title="UN Charter">UN Charter</a>:<sup id="cite_ref-charter_ch2_4-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-charter_ch2-4">[4]</a></sup></p>
<ol>
<li>Membership in the United Nations is open to all peace-loving states which accept the obligations contained in the present Charter and, in the judgement of the Organization, are able and willing to carry out these obligations.</li>
<li>The admission of any such state to membership in the United Nations will be effected by a decision of the General Assembly upon the recommendation of the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council" title="United Nations Security Council">Security Council</a>.</li>
</ol>
<p>A recommendation for admission from the Security Council requires affirmative votes from at least nine of the council's fifteen members, with none of the five <a href="/wiki/Permanent_members_of_the_United_Nations_Security_Council" title="Permanent members of the United Nations Security Council">permanent members</a> using their <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council_veto_power" title="United Nations Security Council veto power">veto power</a>. The Security Council's recommendation must then be approved in the General Assembly by a two-thirds majority vote.<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">[5]</a></sup></p>
<p>In principle, only <a href="/wiki/Sovereign_state" title="Sovereign state">sovereign states</a> can become UN members, and currently all UN members are sovereign states. Although five members were not sovereign when they joined the UN, all subsequently became fully independent between 1946 and 1991. Because a state can only be admitted to membership in the UN by the approval of the Security Council and the General Assembly, <a href="/wiki/List_of_states_with_limited_recognition" title="List of states with limited recognition">a number of states that are considered sovereign</a> according to the <a href="/wiki/Montevideo_Convention" title="Montevideo Convention">Montevideo Convention</a> are not members of the UN. This is because the UN does not consider them to possess <a href="/wiki/Sovereignty" title="Sovereignty">sovereignty</a>, mainly due to the lack of <a href="/wiki/Diplomatic_recognition" title="Diplomatic recognition">international recognition</a> or due to opposition from one of the permanent members.</p>
<p>In addition to the member states, the UN also invites non-member states to become <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_General_Assembly_observers" title="United Nations General Assembly observers">observers at the UN General Assembly</a> (currently two: the <a href="/wiki/Holy_See" title="Holy See">Holy See</a> and <a href="/wiki/State_of_Palestine" title="State of Palestine">Palestine</a>), allowing them to participate and speak in General Assembly meetings, but not vote. Observers are generally <a href="/wiki/Intergovernmental_organization" title="Intergovernmental organization">intergovernmental organizations</a> and international organizations and entities whose statehood or sovereignty is not precisely defined.</p>
<p></p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Original_members">Original members</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Member_states_of_the_United_Nations&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Original members">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:442px;"><a href="/wiki/File:United_Nations_Member_States-1945.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3a/United_Nations_Member_States-1945.png/440px-United_Nations_Member_States-1945.png" width="440" height="191" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3a/United_Nations_Member_States-1945.png/660px-United_Nations_Member_States-1945.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3a/United_Nations_Member_States-1945.png/880px-United_Nations_Member_States-1945.png 2x" data-file-width="1450" data-file-height="628" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:United_Nations_Member_States-1945.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
The United Nations in 1945, after <a href="/wiki/World_War_II" title="World War II">World War II</a>. In light blue, the founding members. In dark blue, protectorates and territories of the founding members.</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:442px;"><a href="/wiki/File:UN_Member_Countries_World.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/15/UN_Member_Countries_World.svg/440px-UN_Member_Countries_World.svg.png" width="440" height="194" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/15/UN_Member_Countries_World.svg/660px-UN_Member_Countries_World.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/15/UN_Member_Countries_World.svg/880px-UN_Member_Countries_World.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="940" data-file-height="415" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:UN_Member_Countries_World.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Map of the current UN member states by their <a href="/wiki/Enlargement_of_the_United_Nations" title="Enlargement of the United Nations">dates of admission</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">[6]</a></sup>
<div class="legend"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color: #5B92E5; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;1945 (original members)</div>
<div class="legend"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color: #008080; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;1946–1959</div>
<div class="legend"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color: #00A24F; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;1960–1989</div>
<div class="legend"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color: #346733; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;1990–present</div>
<div class="legend"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color: #FDE910; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;non-member observer states</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div role="note" class="hatnote">Further information: <a href="/wiki/History_of_the_United_Nations" title="History of the United Nations">History of the United Nations</a></div>
<p>The UN officially came into existence on 24 October 1945, after ratification of the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Charter" title="United Nations Charter">United Nations Charter</a> by the <a href="/wiki/Permanent_members_of_the_United_Nations_Security_Council" title="Permanent members of the United Nations Security Council">five permanent members</a> of the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council" title="United Nations Security Council">United Nations Security Council</a> (the <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_China_(1912-49)" class="mw-redirect" title="Republic of China (1912-49)">Republic of China</a>, <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Soviet_Union" title="Soviet Union">Soviet Union</a>, the <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a>) and a majority of the other signatories.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">[7]</a></sup> A total of 51 original members (or founding members) joined that year; 50 of them signed the Charter at the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Conference_on_International_Organization" title="United Nations Conference on International Organization">United Nations Conference on International Organization</a> in <a href="/wiki/San_Francisco" title="San Francisco">San Francisco</a> on 26 June 1945, while <a href="/wiki/Poland" title="Poland">Poland</a>, which was not represented at the conference, signed it on 15 October 1945.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">[8]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-originalmembers_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-originalmembers-9">[9]</a></sup></p>
<p>The original members of the United Nations were: <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_China_(1912-49)" class="mw-redirect" title="Republic of China (1912-49)">Republic of China</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Soviet_Union" title="Soviet Union">Soviet Union</a>, the <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a>, the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a>, <a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentina</a>, <a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Byelorussian_Soviet_Socialist_Republic" title="Byelorussian Soviet Socialist Republic">Belarus</a>, <a href="/wiki/Belgium" title="Belgium">Belgium</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bolivia" title="Bolivia">Bolivia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazil</a>, <a href="/wiki/Canada" title="Canada">Canada</a>, <a href="/wiki/Chile" title="Chile">Chile</a>, <a href="/wiki/Colombia" title="Colombia">Colombia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Costa_Rica" title="Costa Rica">Costa Rica</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cuba" title="Cuba">Cuba</a>, <a href="/wiki/Czechoslovakia" title="Czechoslovakia">Czechoslovakia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Denmark" title="Denmark">Denmark</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Dominican_Republic" title="Dominican Republic">Dominican Republic</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ecuador" title="Ecuador">Ecuador</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Egypt" title="Kingdom of Egypt">Egypt</a>, <a href="/wiki/El_Salvador" title="El Salvador">El Salvador</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ethiopian_Empire" title="Ethiopian Empire">Ethiopia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Greece" title="Kingdom of Greece">Greece</a>, <a href="/wiki/Guatemala" title="Guatemala">Guatemala</a>, <a href="/wiki/Haiti" title="Haiti">Haiti</a>, <a href="/wiki/Honduras" title="Honduras">Honduras</a>, <a href="/wiki/British_Raj" title="British Raj">India</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pahlavi_dynasty" title="Pahlavi dynasty">Iran</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Iraq" title="Kingdom of Iraq">Iraq</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lebanon" title="Lebanon">Lebanon</a>, <a href="/wiki/Liberia" title="Liberia">Liberia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Luxembourg" title="Luxembourg">Luxembourg</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mexico" title="Mexico">Mexico</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Netherlands" title="Netherlands">Netherlands</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dominion_of_New_Zealand" title="Dominion of New Zealand">New Zealand</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nicaragua" title="Nicaragua">Nicaragua</a>, <a href="/wiki/Norway" title="Norway">Norway</a>, <a href="/wiki/Panama" title="Panama">Panama</a>, <a href="/wiki/Paraguay" title="Paraguay">Paraguay</a>, <a href="/wiki/Peru" title="Peru">Peru</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_of_the_Philippines" title="Commonwealth of the Philippines">Philippines</a>, <a href="/wiki/Polish_People%27s_Republic" title="Polish People's Republic">Poland</a>, <a href="/wiki/Saudi_Arabia" title="Saudi Arabia">Saudi Arabia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Union_of_South_Africa" title="Union of South Africa">South Africa</a>, <a href="/wiki/Syrian_Republic_(1930%E2%80%9358)" title="Syrian Republic (1930–58)">Syria</a>, <a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkey</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ukrainian_Soviet_Socialist_Republic" title="Ukrainian Soviet Socialist Republic">Ukraine</a>, <a href="/wiki/Uruguay" title="Uruguay">Uruguay</a>, <a href="/wiki/Venezuela" title="Venezuela">Venezuela</a> and <a href="/wiki/Yugoslavia" title="Yugoslavia">Yugoslavia</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-originalmembers_9-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-originalmembers-9">[9]</a></sup></p>
<p>Among the original members, 49 are either still UN members or had their memberships in the UN continued by a <a href="/wiki/Succession_of_states" title="Succession of states">successor state</a> <i>(see table below)</i>; for example, the membership of the <a href="/wiki/Soviet_Union" title="Soviet Union">Soviet Union</a> was continued by the <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russian Federation</a> after its dissolution <i>(see the section <a href="#Union_of_Soviet_Socialist_Republics">Former members: Union of Soviet Socialist Republics</a>)</i>. The other two original members, <a href="/wiki/Czechoslovakia" title="Czechoslovakia">Czechoslovakia</a> and <a href="/wiki/Socialist_Federal_Republic_of_Yugoslavia" title="Socialist Federal Republic of Yugoslavia">Yugoslavia</a> (i.e., the Socialist Federal Republic of Yugoslavia), had been dissolved and their memberships in the UN not continued from 1992 by any one successor state <i>(see the sections <a href="#Czechoslovakia">Former members: Czechoslovakia</a> and <a href="#Yugoslavia">Former members: Yugoslavia</a>)</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-originalmembers_9-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-originalmembers-9">[9]</a></sup></p>
<p>At the time of UN's founding, the <a href="/wiki/China_and_the_United_Nations" title="China and the United Nations">seat of China in the UN</a> was held by the <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_China_(1912%E2%80%9349)" title="Republic of China (1912–49)">Republic of China</a>, but as a result of <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_General_Assembly_Resolution_2758" title="United Nations General Assembly Resolution 2758">United Nations General Assembly Resolution 2758</a> in 1971, it is now held by the <a href="/wiki/China" title="China">People's Republic of China</a> <i>(see the section <a href="#Republic_of_China_.28Taiwan.29">Former members: Republic of China (Taiwan)</a>)</i>.</p>
<p>A number of the original members were not sovereign when they joined the UN, and only gained full independence later:<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">[10]</a></sup></p>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Belarus" title="Belarus">Belarus</a> (then the <a href="/wiki/Byelorussian_Soviet_Socialist_Republic" title="Byelorussian Soviet Socialist Republic">Byelorussian Soviet Socialist Republic</a>) and <a href="/wiki/Ukraine" title="Ukraine">Ukraine</a> (then the <a href="/wiki/Ukrainian_Soviet_Socialist_Republic" title="Ukrainian Soviet Socialist Republic">Ukrainian Soviet Socialist Republic</a>) were both <a href="/wiki/Republics_of_the_Soviet_Union" title="Republics of the Soviet Union">constituent republics of the Soviet Union</a>, until gaining full independence in 1991.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/India" title="India">India</a> (whose territory at that time, before the <a href="/wiki/Partition_of_India" title="Partition of India">Partition of India</a>, also included the present-day territories of <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a> and <a href="/wiki/Bangladesh" title="Bangladesh">Bangladesh</a>) was under <a href="/wiki/British_Raj" title="British Raj">British colonial rule</a>, until gaining full independence in 1947.</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a> (then the <a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_of_the_Philippines" title="Commonwealth of the Philippines">Philippine Commonwealth</a>) was a <a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_(U.S._insular_area)" title="Commonwealth (U.S. insular area)">commonwealth with the United States</a>, until gaining full independence in 1946.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/New_Zealand" title="New Zealand">New Zealand</a>, while <i>de facto</i> sovereign at that time, "only gained full capacity to enter into relations with other states in 1947 when it passed the <a href="/wiki/Statute_of_Westminster_Adoption_Act_1947" title="Statute of Westminster Adoption Act 1947">Statute of Westminster Adoption Act</a>. This occurred 16 years after the British Parliament passed the <a href="/wiki/Statute_of_Westminster_1931" title="Statute of Westminster 1931">Statute of Westminster Act</a> in 1931 that recognised New Zealand's autonomy. If judged by the Montevideo Convention criteria, New Zealand did not achieve full <i>de jure</i> statehood until 1947."<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">[11]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Current_members">Current members</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Member_states_of_the_United_Nations&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Current members">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<table role="presentation" class="mbox-small plainlinks sistersitebox" style="background-color:#f9f9f9;border:1px solid #aaa;color:#000">
<tr>
<td class="mbox-image"><a href="/wiki/File:Wikisource-logo.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4c/Wikisource-logo.svg/38px-Wikisource-logo.svg.png" width="38" height="40" class="noviewer" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4c/Wikisource-logo.svg/57px-Wikisource-logo.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4c/Wikisource-logo.svg/76px-Wikisource-logo.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="410" data-file-height="430" /></a></td>
<td class="mbox-text plainlist"><a href="/wiki/Wikisource" title="Wikisource">Wikisource</a> has original text related to this article:
<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/United_Nations_Member_States" class="extiw" title="wikisource:United Nations Member States">United Nations Member States</a></b></div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
<div role="note" class="hatnote">Further information: <a href="/wiki/List_of_sovereign_states" title="List of sovereign states">List of sovereign states</a></div>
<p>The current members and their dates of admission are listed below with their official designations used by the United Nations.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">[12]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">[13]</a></sup></p>
<p>The alphabetical order by the member states' official designations is used to determine the seating arrangement of the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_General_Assembly" title="United Nations General Assembly">General Assembly</a> sessions, where a draw is held each year to select a member state as the starting point.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">[14]</a></sup> Several members use their full official names in their official designations and thus are sorted out of order from their common names: the <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">Democratic People's Republic of Korea</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo" title="Democratic Republic of the Congo">Democratic Republic of the Congo</a>, the <a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">Republic of Korea</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Moldova" title="Moldova">Republic of Moldova</a>, <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Macedonia" title="Republic of Macedonia">The former Yugoslav Republic of Macedonia</a> (a provisional reference used for all purposes within the UN, and listed under T), and the <a href="/wiki/Tanzania" title="Tanzania">United Republic of Tanzania</a>.</p>
<p><i>The member states can be sorted by their official designations and dates of admission by clicking on the buttons in the header of the columns. See related sections on former members by clicking on the links in the column <b>See also</b>.</i></p>
<p>Original members are listed with <span style="background:#ccddff;width:50px;border:1px solid #aaaaaa">blue background</span>.</p>
